1.  Pharmacology: Medical knowledge entry describing diseases,
    mechanisms, symptoms, diagnostics, and treatments. Example concept:
    Hypertension involves chronically elevated arterial blood pressure
    that increases risk of stroke, myocardial infarction, kidney
    disease, and heart failure. Management may include lifestyle
    modification, antihypertensive medications such as ACE inhibitors,
    beta blockers, calcium channel blockers, and diuretics, along with
    continuous monitoring of cardiovascular risk factors.

     disease, and heart failure. Management may include lifestyle
     modification, antihypertensive medications such as ACE inhibitors,
     beta blockers, calcium channel blockers, and diuretics, along with
     continuous monitoring of cardiovascular risk factors.

     Hypertension involves chronically elevated arterial blood pressure
     that increases risk of stroke, myocardial infarction, kidney
     disease, and heart failure. Management may include lifestyle
     modification, antihypertensive medications such as ACE inhibitors,
     beta blockers, calcium channel blockers, and diuretics, along with
     continuous monitoring of cardiovascular risk factors.

     disease, and heart failure. Management may include lifestyle
     modification, antihypertensive medications such as ACE inhibitors,
     beta blockers, calcium channel blockers, and diuretics, along with
     continuous monitoring of cardiovascular risk factors.

     Hypertension involves chronically elevated arterial blood pressure
     that increases risk of stroke, myocardial infarction, kidney
     disease, and heart failure. Management may include lifestyle
     modification, antihypertensive medications such as ACE inhibitors,
     beta blockers, calcium channel blockers, and diuretics, along with
     continuous monitoring of cardiovascular risk factors.
